**Score: 100/100**

| Component | Result | Multiplier |
|-----------|--------|------------|
| Tool call | ✅ Succeeded | 1x |
| Schema validation | ✅ Valid | 1x |
| Azure validation | ✅ Passed | 1x |
| Intent score | 1.00 | 1.00x |

**Intent Justification:**

The resource body correctly specifies East US location, enables soft delete, purge protection, and RBAC authorization, fully matching the user's intent.

**Generated Resource Body:**

```json
{
  "type": "Microsoft.KeyVault/vaults",
  "name": "my-keyvault-eastus",
  "apiVersion": "2023-07-01",
  "location": "eastus",
  "properties": {
    "tenantId": "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
    "sku": {
      "family": "A",
      "name": "standard"
    },
    "enableSoftDelete": true,
    "enablePurgeProtection": true,
    "enableRbacAuthorization": true
  }
}
```

**Score: 100/100**

| Component | Result | Multiplier |
|-----------|--------|------------|
| Tool call | ✅ Succeeded | 1x |
| Schema validation | ✅ Valid | 1x |
| Azure validation | ✅ Passed | 1x |
| Intent score | 1.00 | 1.00x |

**Intent Justification:**

The NSG configuration allows inbound HTTPS (443) from the internet and explicitly denies all other inbound traffic, fully matching the user's intent.

**Generated Resource Body:**

```json
{
  "name": "nsg-https-only",
  "location": "eastus",
  "properties": {
    "securityRules": [
      {
        "name": "Allow-Https-Inbound",
        "properties": {
          "description": "Allow inbound HTTPS traffic from Internet",
          "protocol": "Tcp",
          "sourcePortRange": "*",
          "destinationPortRange": "443",
          "sourceAddressPrefix": "*",
          "destinationAddressPrefix": "*",
          "access": "Allow",
          "priority": 100,
          "direction": "Inbound"
        }
      },
      {
        "name": "Deny-All-Inbound",
        "properties": {
          "description": "Deny all other inbound traffic",
          "protocol": "*",
          "sourcePortRange": "*",
          "destinationPortRange": "*",
          "sourceAddressPrefix": "*",
          "destinationAddressPrefix": "*",
          "access": "Deny",
          "priority": 200,
          "direction": "Inbound"
        }
      }
```

```json
    "details": [
      {
        "code": "SkuNotAvailable",

Please try another size or deploy to a different location or different zone. See https://aka.ms/azureskunotavailable for details."
      }
```

**Intent Justification:**

**Generated Resource Body:**

```json
{
  "name": "myWin2022VM",
  "apiVersion": "2024-03-01",
  "type": "Microsoft.Compute/virtualMachines",
  "location": "[resourceGroup().location]",
  "properties": {
    "hardwareProfile": {
      "vmSize": "Standard_D2s_v5"
    },
    "osProfile": {
      "computerName": "myWin2022VM",
      "adminUsername": "azureuser",
      "adminPassword": "[parameters(\u0027adminPassword\u0027)]"
    },
    "storageProfile": {
      "imageReference": {
        "publisher": "MicrosoftWindowsServer",
        "offer": "WindowsServer",
        "sku": "2022-datacenter-azure-edition",
        "version": "latest"
      },
      "osDisk": {
        "name": "myWin2022VM_OSDisk",
        "caching": "ReadWrite",
        "createOption": "FromImage",
        "managedDisk": {
          "storageAccountType": "StandardSSD_LRS"
        }
      }
    },
    "networkProfile": {
      "networkInterfaces": [
        {
          "id": "[resourceId(\u0027Microsoft.Network/networkInterfaces\u0027, \u0027myWin2022VMNic\u0027)]"
        }
      ]
    },
    "diagnosticsProfile": {
      "bootDiagnostics": {
        "enabled": true,
        "storageUri": "[concat(\u0027https://\u0027, \u0027existingdiagstor\u0027, \u0027.blob.\u0027, environment().suffixes.storage)]"
      }
```
